function PostMessage(msg){
dstWindow.postMessage(msg, 'https://back.ph1.powerboutique.net/maj_471');
}
// fonction qui recupere un message envoyé (par exemple envoyé par la frame du bas lors d'une action qui doit déclancher une evenement dans cette fenetre)
function onMessage(e)
{
// Vous pouvez vÃ©fier l.origine de la fenÃªe avec e.origin
//document.getElementById('div-test').innerHTML = e.data;
if(e.origin.indexOf("https://back.ph1.powerboutique.net/maj_471" != 0)){
eval(e.data);
}
}
// capter les evenements de type message

function getFichierCourant(){
var fichierCourant = "index";
return fichierCourant;

//creer un div surbrillance
var marqueur = document.createElement('div');
marqueur.setAttribute("id","idMarqueur");
marqueur.setAttribute("class","marqueur");
function position(e){
x = (navigator.appName.substring(0,3) == "Net") ? e.pageX : event.x+document.body.scrollLeft;
y = (navigator.appName.substring(0,3) == "Net") ? e.pageY : event.y+document.body.scrollTop;
window.status = "Souris X:"+x+" / Y:"+y;
}
function dragStart(event) {
if(event.target.getAttribute('class').indexOf("dragPointer")!= -1){
event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
event.dataTransfer.setData("Text", event.target.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.getAttribute('id'));
}
}
function dragOver(event) {
var elementConteneur = event.target;
while(elementConteneur.className != "conteneur" && elementConteneur.className != "conteneurAbsolu"){
elementPosition = elementConteneur;
elementConteneur = elementConteneur.parentNode;
}
if(elementConteneur.className == "conteneur"){
try{
// mettre en surbrillance l'endroit ou le bloc va etre droppe
marqueur.setAttribute("class","marqueur");
//if(elementConteneur.childNodes.length > 3)
if(elementConteneur.childNodes.length > 3){
elementConteneur.insertBefore(marqueur,elementPosition);
}
else{
elementConteneur.appendChild(marqueur);
}
}
catch(err)
{
}
}
else{
if(event.dataTransfer.getData("Text").indexOf("dragcms")!= -1){
elementConteneur.style.border = "1px solid #FE0000";
}
}
return false;
}
function dragLeave(event) {
var elementConteneur = event.target;
while(elementConteneur.className != "conteneur" && elementConteneur.className != "conteneurAbsolu"){
elementPosition = elementConteneur;
elementConteneur = elementConteneur.parentNode;
}
//elementConteneur.style.border = "";
//elementConteneur.removeChild(marqueur);
// enlever la subrillance de la zone ou le bloc va etre droppe
marqueur.setAttribute("class","marqueurMasque");
if(elementConteneur.className != "conteneur" && elementConteneur.className != "conteneurAbsolu"){
elementConteneur.removeChild(marqueur);
}
return false;
}
function drop(event) {
event.stopPropagation();
marqueur.style.height = "0px";
var elementConteneur = event.target;
while(elementConteneur.className != "conteneur" && elementConteneur.className != "conteneurAbsolu"){
elementPosition = elementConteneur;
elementConteneur = elementConteneur.parentNode;
}
var element = event.dataTransfer.getData("Text");
if (element != "") {
if (! (element = document.getElementById(element))) {
return false;
}
} else {
return false
}
if( elementConteneur.className == "conteneurAbsolu" ){
var coordTop = (event.clientY + document.documentElement.scrollTop) - elementConteneur.offsetTop + "px";
var coordLeft = (event.clientX + document.documentElement.scrollLeft) - elementConteneur.offsetLeft + "px";
/*var coordTop = event.clientY - elementConteneur.offsetTop + "px";
var coordLeft = event.clientX - elementConteneur.offsetLeft + "px";*/
elementConteneur.appendChild(element);
element.style.position="absolute";
element.style.top=coordTop;
element.style.left=coordLeft;
}
else{
element.style.top="";
element.style.left="";
//if(elementConteneur.childNodes.length > 2)
if(elementConteneur.childNodes.length > 0){
elementConteneur.insertBefore(element,elementPosition);
}
else{
elementConteneur.appendChild(element);
}
}
boolModif = true;
//parent.recherche.document.getElementById('boutonSave').disabled = false;
//parent.recherche.document.getElementById('boutonSave').className = "bouton bouton_save";
PostMessage('document.getElementById("boutonSave").disabled = false');
PostMessage('document.getElementById("boutonSave").className = "bouton bouton_save"');
return false;
}
function afficheTableau(){
boolModif = false;
var myForm = document.createElement('form');
myForm.setAttribute("action","https://back.ph1.powerboutique.net/maj_471/administration/loading.cfm");
myForm.setAttribute("method","post");
var conteneurArray = document.getElementsByClassName("conteneur");
for(i=0;i<conteneurArray.length;i++){
if(typeof(conteneurArray[i].id)!='undefined')
{
var name = conteneurArray[i].id;
var value = "";
//sortie = sortie + conteneurArray[i].id + "\n";
var dragArray = conteneurArray[i].getElementsByClassName("draggableBox");
for(j=0;j<dragArray.length;j++){
if(typeof(dragArray[j].id)!='undefined')
{
value = value + "*" + dragArray[j].id + "*";
}
}
var myElement = document.createElement("input");
myElement.setAttribute("type","hidden");
myElement.setAttribute("name",name);
myElement.setAttribute("value",value);
myForm.appendChild(myElement);
}
}
conteneurAbs = document.getElementsByClassName("conteneurAbsolu");
if(conteneurAbs.length > 0){
var dragArray = conteneurAbs[0].getElementsByClassName("draggableBox");
var name = conteneurAbs[0].id;
var value = "";
for(j=0;j<dragArray.length;j++){
if(typeof(dragArray[j].id)!='undefined')
{
if(value != ""){
value += ",";
}
value = value + "*" + dragArray[j].id + "*";
}
}
}
var myElement = document.createElement("input");
myElement.setAttribute("type","hidden");
//myElement.setAttribute("name",name);
myElement.setAttribute("name",'conteneurAbsolu');
myElement.setAttribute("value",value);
myForm.appendChild(myElement);
// gestion des coord pour les positionnements absolus
for(j=0;j<dragArray.length;j++){
if(typeof(dragArray[j].id)!='undefined'){
if(dragArray[j].style.top != "" && dragArray[j].style.left != ""){
var myElement = document.createElement("input");
myElement.setAttribute("type","hidden");
myElement.setAttribute("name","coordx"+dragArray[j].id);
myElement.setAttribute("value",dragArray[j].style.top);
myForm.appendChild(myElement);
var myElement = document.createElement("input");
myElement.setAttribute("type","hidden");
myElement.setAttribute("name","coordy"+dragArray[j].id);
myElement.setAttribute("value",dragArray[j].style.left);
myForm.appendChild(myElement);
}
}
}
var myElement = document.createElement("input");
myElement.setAttribute("type","hidden");
myElement.setAttribute("name","fichierCourant");
myElement.setAttribute("value","index");
myForm.appendChild(myElement);
document.body.appendChild(myForm);
var myElement = document.createElement("input");
myElement.setAttribute("type","hidden");
myElement.setAttribute("name","codeLg");
myElement.setAttribute("value","lg_fr");
myForm.appendChild(myElement);
var myElement = document.createElement("input");
myElement.setAttribute("type","hidden");
myElement.setAttribute("id","idSite");
myElement.setAttribute("name","idSite");
myElement.setAttribute("value","1");
myForm.appendChild(myElement);
myForm.submit();
}

if((window.parent.recherche) && (window.parent.resultat)) {
onload = function() {
var conteneurArray1 = document.getElementsByClassName("conteneur");
var conteneurArray2 = document.getElementsByClassName("conteneurAbsolu");
for(i=0;i<conteneurArray1.length;i++){
conteneurArray1[i].setAttribute('ondragstart','dragStart(event);');
conteneurArray1[i].setAttribute('ondragover','return dragOver(event);');
conteneurArray1[i].setAttribute('ondragleave','return dragLeave(event);');
conteneurArray1[i].setAttribute('ondrop','return drop(event);');
conteneurArray1[i].setAttribute('id','conteneur'+i);
conteneurArray1[i].setAttribute('style','border:1px solid #CCC;padding:2px;');
}
for(i=0;i<conteneurArray2.length;i++){
conteneurArray2[i].setAttribute('ondragstart','dragStart(event);');
conteneurArray2[i].setAttribute('ondragover','return dragOver(event);');
conteneurArray2[i].setAttribute('ondragleave','return dragLeave(event);');
conteneurArray2[i].setAttribute('ondrop','return drop(event);');
conteneurArray2[i].setAttribute('style','position:relative;border:1px solid #CCC;padding:2px;');

document.getElementById(parent.recherche.idBlocNew).style.backgroundColor = "lightgreen";
}*/

}

if(boolModif){
//parent.recherche.document.getElementById('boutonSave').className = "bouton bouton_save_alerte";
PostMessage('document.getElementById("boutonSave").className = "bouton bouton_save_alerte"');

message += "Pour enregistrer, vous devez cliquer sur le bouton 'Annuler' de cette fenêtre, puis sur le bouton 'Enregistrer la position des blocs' en haut de page.\n";

evt = window.event;
}
if (evt) {
evt.returnValue = message;
}
return message;
}
}

}

function getOpacite(id,mode){
var classOpacite = "opacite";
if (mode == "on"){
classOpacite = "";
}
if(document.getElementById('deplacer'+id)){
document.getElementById('deplacer'+id).className = "dragPointer boutonWysiwyg "+classOpacite;
}
if(document.getElementById('modifier'+id)){
document.getElementById('modifier'+id).className = "boutonWysiwyg "+classOpacite;
}
if(document.getElementById('activer'+id)){
document.getElementById('activer'+id).className = "boutonWysiwyg "+classOpacite;
}
if(document.getElementById('supprimer'+id)){
document.getElementById('supprimer'+id).className = "boutonWysiwyg "+classOpacite;
}
}
